namespace = dg_catholic
province_event = {
	id = dg_catholic.001
	title = dg_catholic.001.t
	desc = dg_catholic.001.d
	picture = catholic_simony
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_year = 1380
				}
				NOT = {
					AVI = {
						num_of_cities = 1
						AND = {
							OR = {
								has_reform = papacy_reform
								has_reform = papal_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				owner = {
					add_reform_desire = 0.001
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								is_religion_enabled = protestant
							}
						}
						PAP = {
							change_variable = {
								which = reform_desire_simony
								value = 0.1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_year = 1380
					AVI = {
						num_of_cities = 1
						AND = {
							OR = {
								has_reform = papacy_reform
								has_reform = papal_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							adm_tech = 12
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_year = 1510
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				owner = {
					add_reform_desire = 0.001
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								is_religion_enabled = protestant
							}
						}
						PAP = {
							change_variable = {
								which = reform_desire_simony
								value = 0.1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					AND = {
						adm_tech = 12
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_year = 1510
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 75
				owner = {
					add_reform_desire = 0.001
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								is_religion_enabled = protestant
							}
						}
						PAP = {
							change_variable = {
								which = reform_desire_simony
								value = 0.1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_year = 1510
			}
			owner = {
				add_reform_desire = 0.001
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_religion_enabled = protestant
						}
					}
					PAP = {
						change_variable = {
							which = reform_desire_simony
							value = 0.1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = renaissance
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							has_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation
						}
					}
				}
				owner = {
					change_variable = {
						which = catholic_corruption
						value = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							num_of_cities = 12
						}
					}
					owner = {
						change_variable = {
							which = catholic_corruption
							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							num_of_cities = 48
						}
					}
					owner = {
						change_variable = {
							which = catholic_corruption
							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = greedy_bishop
			duration = 2000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					num_of_cities = 12
				}
			}
			owner = {
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						area = ROOT
						NOT = {
							province_id = ROOT
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_modifier = effective_bishop
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler
						}
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = greedy_bishop
						duration = 2000
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					num_of_cities = 48
				}
			}
			owner = {
				random_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						region = ROOT
						NOT = {
							area = ROOT
						}
						NOT = {
							province_id = ROOT
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_modifier = effective_bishop
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler
						}
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = greedy_bishop
						duration = 2000
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.001.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					check_variable = {
						which = inquisition
						value = 1
					}
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = humanism
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						capital_distance = {
							who = PAP
							distance = 130
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.7
				owner = {
					capital_distance = {
						who = PAP
						distance = 260
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = renaissance
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
						has_province_modifier = catholic_archbishopric
						value = 3
					}
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = ally_of_pope
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = friend_of_pope
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = rival_of_pope
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = simony
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_province_flag = simony_province
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					has_province_flag = simony_province
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
					}
					set_province_flag = simony_province
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = simony
		}
		PAP = {
			add_treasury = 5
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					culture = PREV
					has_owner_culture = yes
					owner = {
						religion = catholic
						NOT = {
							num_of_cities = 12
						}
						ai = yes
					}
				}
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = simony
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.001.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					num_of_cardinals = 1
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					num_of_cardinals = 3
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					num_of_cardinals = 6
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
					}
					set_province_flag = simony_province
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					DIP = 6
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 90
				owner = {
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
							OR = {
								province_id = ROOT
								area = ROOT
							}
						}
						remove_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					DIP = 5
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 75
				owner = {
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
							OR = {
								province_id = ROOT
								area = ROOT
							}
						}
						remove_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					DIP = 4
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 60
				owner = {
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
							OR = {
								province_id = ROOT
								area = ROOT
							}
						}
						remove_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					DIP = 3
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 45
				owner = {
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
							OR = {
								province_id = ROOT
								area = ROOT
							}
						}
						remove_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					DIP = 2
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 30
				owner = {
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
							OR = {
								province_id = ROOT
								area = ROOT
							}
						}
						remove_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				chance = 15
				owner = {
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
							OR = {
								province_id = ROOT
								area = ROOT
							}
						}
						remove_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					culture_group = PREV
					has_owner_culture = yes
					owner = {
						religion = catholic
						ai = yes
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = simony
						}
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = neighbor_complaint
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					culture_group = PREV
					has_owner_culture = yes
					owner = {
						religion = catholic
						ai = yes
					}
				}
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = simony
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_papal_influence = -5
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = simony
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = PAP
				modifier = reform_demands_minor
			}
		}
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = dg_catholic.002
	title = dg_catholic.002.t
	desc = dg_catholic.002.d
	picture = catholic_corrupt_priest
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_year = 1380
				}
				NOT = {
					AVI = {
						num_of_cities = 1
						AND = {
							OR = {
								has_reform = papacy_reform
								has_reform = papal_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				owner = {
					add_reform_desire = 0.001
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								is_religion_enabled = protestant
							}
						}
						PAP = {
							change_variable = {
								which = reform_desire_absenteeism
								value = 0.1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_year = 1380
					AVI = {
						num_of_cities = 1

							OR = {

								which = reform_desire_absenteeism
								value = 0.1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

			limit = {
				owner = {
					AND = {
						adm_tech = 12
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_year = 1510
				}
			}
			random = {

				add_reform_desire = 0.001
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_religion_enabled = protestant
						}
					}
					PAP = {
						change_variable = {
							which = reform_desire_absenteeism
							value = 0.1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = renaissance
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							has_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation
						}
					}
				}
				owner = {
					change_variable = {

					}
				}
				if = {

	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.002.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					owner = {
						piety = -0.20
					}
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					check_variable = {
						which = inquisition
						value = 1
					}
				}
				factor = 1.2
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = humanism
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = absenteeism
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_province_flag = absentee_bishop
				factor = 0.5

			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = ally_of_pope
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {

					has_country_flag = friend_of_pope
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = rival_of_pope
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = enemy_of_pope
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						piety = -0.20
					}
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = absentee_bishop
				duration = 1000
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						num_of_cities = 12
					}
				}
				owner = {
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							area = ROOT
							NOT = {
								province_id = ROOT
							}
							OR = {
								AND = {
									OR = {
										has_terrain = jungle_flats
										has_terrain = jungle_hills
									}
								}
								AND = {
									OR = {
										has_terrain = desert_flats
										has_terrain = desert_hills
										has_terrain = desert_mountains
										has_terrain = desert_highlands
									}
								}
								AND = {
									OR = {
										has_terrain = forest_mountains
										has_terrain = wood_mountains
										has_terrain = shrub_mountains
										has_terrain = grass_mountains
										has_terrain = desert_mountains
										has_terrain = alpine_tundra
									}
								}
								has_terrain = marsh
								AND = {
									OR = {
										has_terrain = forest_highlands
										has_terrain = wood_highlands
										has_terrain = shrub_highlands
										has_terrain = grass_highlands
										has_terrain = desert_highlands
									}
								}
								AND = {
									OR = {
										has_terrain = grass_flats
										has_terrain = grass_hills
									}
									OR = {
										region = steppes_region
										superregion = central_asia_superregion
									}
								}
								NOT = {
									development = 5
								}
							}
							NOT = {
								has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
							}
							NOT = {
								has_province_modifier = effective_bishop
							}
							NOT = {
								has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop
							}
							NOT = {
								has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler
							}
						}
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = absentee_bishop
							duration = 1000
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						num_of_cities = 48
					}
				}
				owner = {
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							region = ROOT
							NOT = {
								area = ROOT
							}
							NOT = {
								province_id = ROOT
							}
							OR = {
								AND = {
									OR = {
										has_terrain = jungle_flats
										has_terrain = jungle_hills
									}
								}
								AND = {
									OR = {
										has_terrain = desert_flats
										has_terrain = desert_hills
										has_terrain = desert_mountains
										has_terrain = desert_highlands
									}
								}
								AND = {
									OR = {
										has_terrain = forest_mountains
										has_terrain = wood_mountains
										has_terrain = shrub_mountains
										has_terrain = grass_mountains

									}
								}
								NOT = {
									development = 5
								}
							}
							NOT = {
								has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
							}
							NOT = {
								has_province_modifier = effective_bishop
							}
							NOT = {
								has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop
							}
							NOT = {
								has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler

province_event = {
	id = dg_catholic.003
	title = dg_catholic.003.t
	desc = dg_catholic.003.d
	picture = catholic_papal_nepotism
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_year = 1380
				}
				NOT = {
					AVI = {
						num_of_cities = 1
						AND = {
							OR = {
								has_reform = papacy_reform
								has_reform = papal_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				owner = {
					add_reform_desire = 0.001
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								is_religion_enabled = protestant
							}
						}
						PAP = {
							change_variable = {
								which = reform_desire_clerical_corruption
								value = 0.1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_year = 1380
					AVI = {
						num_of_cities = 1
						AND = {
							OR = {
								has_reform = papacy_reform
								has_reform = papal_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							adm_tech = 12
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_year = 1510
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				owner = {
					add_reform_desire = 0.001
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								is_religion_enabled = protestant
							}
						}
						PAP = {
							change_variable = {
								which = reform_desire_clerical_corruption
								value = 0.1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					AND = {
						adm_tech = 12
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_year = 1510
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 75
				owner = {
					add_reform_desire = 0.001
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								is_religion_enabled = protestant
							}
						}
						PAP = {
							change_variable = {
								which = reform_desire_clerical_corruption
								value = 0.1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_year = 1510
			}
			owner = {
				add_reform_desire = 0.001
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_religion_enabled = protestant
						}
					}
					PAP = {
						change_variable = {
							which = reform_desire_clerical_corruption
							value = 0.1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = renaissance
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							has_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation
						}
					}
				}
				owner = {
					change_variable = {
						which = catholic_corruption
						value = 1
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							num_of_cities = 12
						}
					}
					owner = {
						change_variable = {
							which = catholic_corruption
							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							num_of_cities = 48
						}
					}
					owner = {
						change_variable = {
							which = catholic_corruption
							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				set_country_flag = papal_nepotism
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.003.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = religious_scandal_province
			duration = 5000
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.003.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				PAP = {
					has_country_flag = reformer_pope
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = national_church
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = patronato_real
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					is_papal_controller = yes
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					PAP = {
						has_country_flag = reformer_pope
					}
					owner = {
						has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction
					}
					owner = {
						has_country_flag = national_church
					}
					owner = {
						has_country_flag = patronato_real
					}
					owner = {
						is_papal_controller = yes
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				add_dip_power = -10
			}
		}
		else = {
			owner = {
				add_dip_power = -20
				add_papal_influence = -5
			}
		}
	}
}

				chance = 75
				add_reform_desire = 0.001
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								is_religion_enabled = protestant
							}
						}
						PAP = {
							change_variable = {
								which = reform_desire_popular_piety
								value = 0.1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_year = 1510
			}
			add_reform_desire = 0.001
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_religion_enabled = protestant
						}
					}
					PAP = {
						change_variable = {
							which = reform_desire_popular_piety
							value = 0.1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = catholic_popular_piety
		add_piety = 0.10
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.006.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		add_papal_influence = -10
		set_country_flag = catholic_anticlericalism
		add_piety = -0.10
	}
}

						who = ROOT
						distance = 390
					}

				factor = 1.4
			}

					}

			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 10
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 20
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				num_of_cities = 30
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = excommunicated
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = great_matter
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = papal_interference
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = conciliarism_suppressed
		reverse_add_opinion = {
			who = PAP
			modifier = obeyed_religious_leader
		}
		add_papal_influence = 5
		if = {
			limit = {
				advisor = theologian
			}
			remove_advisor = theologian
			add_patriarch_authority = -0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.80
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unhappy_church_powerful
				duration = 500
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.60
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unhappy_church_strong
				duration = 500
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.40
			}

				duration = 500
			}
		}

			}

				name = unhappy_church_weak
				duration = 500
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = unhappy_church_impotent
				duration = 500
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = dg_catholic.011
	title = ai_only.t
	desc = ai_only.d
	picture = ai_only
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		religion = catholic
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = minority_timer_catholic
		}
		OR = {
			piety = -0.60
			PAP = {
				check_variable = {
					which = papal_authority
					value = 400
				}
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 25
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.60
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.20
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = minority_timer_catholic
			duration = 300
			hidden = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = catholic_event
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_only.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_reform = papacy_reform
							has_reform = papal_government
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = national_church
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = patronato_real
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = catholic_event
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = catholic_popular_piety
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = catholic_anticlericalism
					}
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = counter_reformation
					}
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = absenteeism
						has_country_flag = simony
						has_country_flag = indulgences_condemned
						has_country_flag = royal_scandal
						has_country_flag = canonical_court_scandal
						AVI = {
							AND = {
								OR = {
									has_reform = papacy_reform
									has_reform = papal_government
								}
							}
							num_of_cities = 1
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = catholic_event
						has_country_flag = absenteeism
					}
					random = {
						chance = 6
						clr_country_flag = catholic_event
						country_event = {
							id = dg_catholic.006
							days = 0
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = catholic_event
						has_country_flag = simony
					}
					random = {
						chance = 6
						clr_country_flag = catholic_event
						country_event = {
							id = dg_catholic.006
							days = 0
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = catholic_event
						has_country_flag = indulgences_condemned
					}
					random = {
						chance = 6
						clr_country_flag = catholic_event
						country_event = {
							id = dg_catholic.006
							days = 0
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = catholic_event
						has_country_flag = royal_scandal
					}
					random = {
						chance = 6
						clr_country_flag = catholic_event
						country_event = {
							id = dg_catholic.006
							days = 0
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = catholic_event
						has_country_flag = canonical_court_scandal
					}
					random = {
						chance = 6
						clr_country_flag = catholic_event
						country_event = {
							id = dg_catholic.006
							days = 0
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = catholic_event
					PAP = {
						has_country_flag = indulgences_permitted
					}
					PAP = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = indulgences_banned
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						government = theocracy
					}
					any_owned_province = {
						continent = europe
						religion = catholic
						NOT = {
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_modifier = effective_bishop
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler
						}
						NOT = {
							has_province_modifier = religious_scandal_province
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = catholic_event
						OR = {
							has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_strong
							has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country
							has_country_modifier = religious_scandal_country_weak

								}
							}

										id = stacking_unrest.002
									}
								}
							}

						}

							}
							add_prestige = -1
							add_country_modifier = {
								name = anticlericalism
								duration = 100
							}

							}

									}

									}

									}

										piety = -0.20
									}
								}
								add_province_modifier = {
									name = catholic_pilgrimage
									duration = 3000
								}
							}
							else = {
								add_province_modifier = {
									name = catholic_pilgrimage
									duration = 1500
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = catholic_event
	}

			has_country_flag = excommunicated
		}

			has_country_flag = sainthood_candidate
		}
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_reform = papacy_reform
					has_reform = papal_government
				}
			}
		}
		piety = -0.60
		OR = {
			ai = yes
			has_country_flag = religious_news_major
		}
	}

		}

	desc = dg_catholic.024.d
	picture = catholic_bishop
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_province_flag = effective_bishop
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						num_of_cities = 72
					}
				}
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						area = ROOT
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = effective_bishop
						}
					}
					set_province_flag = effective_bishop
				}
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						NOT = {
							area = ROOT
						}
						region = ROOT
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = effective_bishop
						}
					}
					set_province_flag = effective_bishop
				}
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						NOT = {
							area = ROOT
						}
						region = ROOT
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = effective_bishop
						}
					}
					set_province_flag = effective_bishop
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						num_of_cities = 24
					}
				}
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						area = ROOT
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = effective_bishop
						}
					}
					set_province_flag = effective_bishop
				}
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						NOT = {
							area = ROOT
						}
						region = ROOT
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = effective_bishop
						}
					}
					set_province_flag = effective_bishop
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						num_of_cities = 8
					}
				}
				random_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = ROOT
						area = ROOT
						NOT = {
							has_province_flag = effective_bishop
						}
					}
					set_province_flag = effective_bishop
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.024.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		owner = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_flag = effective_bishop
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = effective_bishop
					duration = 8000
				}
				remove_province_modifier = religious_scandal_province
				remove_province_modifier = absentee_bishop
				remove_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
				remove_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler
				clr_province_flag = effective_bishop
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.024.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					num_of_loans = 1
				}
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					is_bankrupt = yes
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				owner = {
					any_owned_province = {
						any_neighbor_province = {
							has_province_flag = effective_bishop
						}
						OR = {
							has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop
							has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
							has_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler
							has_province_modifier = religious_scandal_province
						}
					}
				}
				factor = 3
			}
		}
		owner = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_province_flag = effective_bishop
						any_neighbor_province = {
							has_province_flag = effective_bishop
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_province_flag = effective_bishop
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = effective_bishop
						duration = 8000
					}
				}
				remove_province_modifier = religious_scandal_province
				remove_province_modifier = absentee_bishop
				remove_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
				remove_province_modifier = indulgence_peddler
				clr_province_flag = effective_bishop
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					monthly_income = 100
				}
				add_treasury = -50
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					monthly_income = 10
				}
				add_years_of_income = -0.04
			}
			else = {
				add_treasury = -5
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				owner = {
					define_advisor = {
						religion = catholic
						culture = ROOT
						type = theologian
						discount = yes
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				owner = {
					define_advisor = {
						religion = catholic
						culture = ROOT
						type = inquisitor
						discount = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = dg_catholic.025
	title = dg_catholic.025.t
	desc = dg_catholic.025.d
	picture = catholic_bishop
	trigger = {
		owner = {
			NOT = {
				tag = PAP
			}
		}
		OR = {
			is_capital = yes
			has_province_modifier = effective_bishop
		}
		AND = {
			base_production = 5
		}
		OR = {
			continent = europe
			AND = {
				base_production = 10
			}
		}
		owner = {
			religion = catholic
		}
		OR = {
			owner = {
				num_of_cities = 10
			}
			AND = {
				superregion = italy_superregion
				has_owner_culture = yes
			}
		}
		owner = {
			NOT = {
				war_with = PAP
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = excommunicated
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = hiding_luther
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = sheltered_luther
			}
			piety = -0.60
			patriarch_authority = 0.40
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
			}
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				has_country_flag = religious_news_major
			}
		}
		OR = {
			is_capital = yes
			AND = {
				superregion = italy_superregion
				has_owner_culture = yes
				AND = {
					base_production = 10
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						has_province_flag = catholic_archbishopric
					}
				}
			}
		}
		any_neighbor_province = {
			owner = {
				religion = catholic
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_flag = catholic_archbishopric
		}
		NOT = {
			has_province_modifier = absentee_bishop
		}
		is_core = owner
		controlled_by = owner
		has_siege = no
		has_global_flag = living_pope
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 83
		modifier = {
			is_capital = yes
			has_province_modifier = effective_bishop
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				is_in_capital_area = yes
			}
			factor = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_modifier = greedy_bishop
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.80
			}
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.60
			}
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					patriarch_authority = 0.40
				}
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					patriarch_authority = 0.20
				}
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = {
				num_of_cardinals = 3
			}
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = {
				num_of_cardinals = 6
			}
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			owner = {
				num_of_cardinals = 9
			}
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				religion = catholic
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			has_province_modifier = catholic_prelate
			factor = 0.5
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.025.a
		set_province_flag = catholic_archbishopric
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = catholic_archbishopric
			duration = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_building = temple
							has_building = temple_heathen
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_building = great_temple
					}
				}
				num_free_building_slots = 1
			}
			add_building = temple
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					religion = catholic
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = {
					which = province_religion
					value = -4
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = catholic
					value = 4
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = catholic_10
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_prestige = 4
				add_papal_influence = 8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_prestige = 3
				add_papal_influence = 6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_prestige = 2
				add_papal_influence = 4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_prestige = 1
				add_papal_influence = 2
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = dg_catholic.026
	title = dg_catholic.026.t
	desc = dg_catholic.026.d
	picture = catholic_papal_legate
	trigger = {
		religion = catholic
		OR = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.60
			PAP = {
				check_variable = {
					which = papal_authority
					value = 400
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			any_neighbor_country = {
				has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = excommunicated
		}
		exists = PAP
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_reform = papacy_reform
					has_reform = papal_government
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction
		}
		any_neighbor_country = {
			religion = catholic
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = excommunicated
			}
			ai = yes
			NOT = {
				war_with = ROOT
			}
			NOT = {
				vassal_of = ROOT
			}
			NOT = {
				overlord_of = ROOT
			}
			NOT = {
				junior_union_with = ROOT
			}
			NOT = {
				senior_union_with = ROOT
			}
			NOT = {
				stability = 2
			}
			NOT = {
				has_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					value = 50
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = catholic_pragmatic_sanction
			}
			OR = {
				overextension_percentage = 0.25
				num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 1

				trade_embargo_by = ROOT

		}

			ai = yes
			has_country_flag = religious_news_major
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 416

					}
				}
			}
			factor = 2
		}

				AND = {

			}

		}
	}
	immediate = {
		random_neighbor_country = {

					}
				}
				NOT = {

				}
				OR = {
					overextension_percentage = 0.25
					num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 1
					truce_with = ROOT
					culture_group = ROOT
					trade_embargo_by = ROOT
					is_rival = ROOT
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = aggrieved_party
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = grievance
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
						OR = {
							truce_with = ROOT
							overextension_percentage = 0.25
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = grievance_military
				random_neighbor_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
					}
					set_country_flag = grievance_military
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						any_owned_province = {
							has_province_modifier = center_of_trade_modifier
						}
						any_neighbor_country = {
							has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
							OR = {
								any_owned_province = {
									has_province_modifier = center_of_trade_modifier
								}
								trade_embargo_by = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = grievance_trade

					}

				}
			}
			else_if = {

				piety = -0.60

			add_republican_tradition = 1

		else = {
			add_legitimacy = 1
			add_devotion = 2
			add_republican_tradition = 0.5
		}
		add_prestige = 5
	}

		}

						}
					}
					is_papal_controller = yes
				}
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = papacy_great
			}
		}
		random_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = aggrieved_party
			}
			set_country_flag = lenient_ruling
			remove_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = grievance
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = PAP
				modifier = papacy_bad
			}
			country_event = {
				id = dg_catholic.028
				days = 30
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = arbitration_bribe
				value = 0
			}
			clr_country_flag = grievance_diplomatic
			clr_country_flag = grievance_military
			clr_country_flag = grievance_trade
		}
	}

province_event = {
	id = dg_catholic.301
	title = dg_catholic.301.t
	desc = dg_catholic.301.d
	picture = catholic_reliquary_saffron
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		check_variable = {
			which = christian_relics
			value = 1
		}
		NOT = {
			controlled_by = owner
		}
		controller = {
			religion_group = christian
			NOT = {
				religion = reformed
			}
			NOT = {
				religion = protestant
			}
			piety = -0.60
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 25
		modifier = {
			controller = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			controller = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			controller = {
				NOT = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
			}
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ai_only.a
		controller = {
			country_event = {
				id = dg_catholic.302
				days = 0
			}
		}
		remove_province_modifier = catholic_pilgrimage
		remove_province_modifier = coptic_pilgrimage
		remove_province_modifier = pilgrimage_route
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = christian
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = christian_relics
						value = 5
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_unrest
					duration = 500
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_variable_equal = {
						which = christian_relics
						value = 4
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_unrest
					duration = 400
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_variable_equal = {
						which = christian_relics
						value = 3
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_unrest
					duration = 300
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_variable_equal = {
						which = christian_relics
						value = 2
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_unrest
					duration = 200
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_variable_equal = {
						which = christian_relics
						value = 1
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_unrest
					duration = 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = dg_catholic.303
	title = dg_catholic.303.t
	desc = dg_catholic.303.d
	picture = catholic_reliquary_saffron
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = papal_fiefdom_ENG
		OR = {
			tag = ENG
			tag = GBR
		}

		NOT = {
			is_papal_controller = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.303.never
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					papal_influence = 1
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					prestige = 0
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				any_rival_country = {
					is_papal_controller = yes
				}
				factor = 2
			}
		}
		add_papal_influence = -10
		reverse_add_opinion = {
			who = PAP
			modifier = disobeyed_religious_leader
		}
		add_prestige = 10
		clr_country_flag = papal_fiefdom_ENG
		set_country_flag = papal_interference
	}
	option = {

				NOT = {

				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					treasury = 50
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {

			name = jesuit_schools
			duration = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = monastic_schools
			}
			remove_country_modifier = monastic_schools
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = charity_schools
			}
			remove_country_modifier = charity_schools
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.05
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = dg_public_schools
			}
			remove_country_modifier = dg_public_schools
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = preparatory_schools
			}
			remove_country_modifier = preparatory_schools
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.10
		}
		else = {
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.10
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.035.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				factor = 1.4
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = dg_catholic.044
	title = dg_catholic.044.t
	desc = dg_catholic.044.d
	picture = catholic_crusade
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.044.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_papal_controller = yes
					tag = PAP
				}
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = papacy_great
			}
		}
		add_yearly_manpower = 1
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_war_exhaustion = -4
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = morale_boost
					duration = 800
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_war_exhaustion = -3
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = morale_boost
					duration = 600
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_war_exhaustion = -2
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = morale_boost
					duration = 400
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_war_exhaustion = -1
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = morale_boost
					duration = 200
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_war_exhaustion = -1
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = morale_boost
				duration = 200
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = dg_catholic.046
	title = dg_catholic.046.t
	desc = dg_catholic.046.d
	picture = catholic_crusade_successful
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = crusade_sponsor
		OR = {
			PAP = {
				check_variable = {
					which = crusade_manpower
					value = 1
				}
			}
			PAP = {
				check_variable = {
					which = crusade_funding
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_modifier = crusade_hub
			}
		}
		OR = {
			at_war_with_religious_enemy = yes
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = internal_crusade
				num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 1
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 10
		modifier = {

			}

					}

				factor = 1.4
			}
		}

			}

province_event = {
	id = dg_catholic.057
	title = dg_catholic.057.t
	desc = dg_catholic.057.d
	picture = catholic_church_trial
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = church_council
		NOT = {
			has_province_modifier = church_council
		}
		NOT = {
			PAP = {
				has_country_flag = council_accomplishments
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			PAP = {
				clr_country_flag = church_council_topics_chosen
				clr_country_flag = council_site_chosen
				clr_country_flag = church_council
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.057.a
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_province_flag = church_council
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_prestige = -3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_prestige = -2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_prestige = -1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = attend_council
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.60
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = council_failed_fanatical
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.20
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = council_failed_pious
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.20
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = council_failed_observant
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = attend_council
			}
			PAP = {
				clr_country_flag = council_accomplishments
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
					OR = {
						is_papal_controller = yes
						tag = PAP
						AND = {
							religion = catholic
							has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = dg_catholic.111
					days = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = dg_catholic.059
	title = dg_catholic.059.t
	desc = dg_catholic.059.d
	picture = catholic_church_council
	trigger = {
		has_province_flag = church_council
		has_province_modifier = church_council
		OR = {
			has_siege = yes
			NOT = {
				controlled_by = owner
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				has_siege = yes
			}
			any_neighbor_province = {
				controlled_by = REB
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12
		modifier = {
			has_siege = yes
			factor = 0.2
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				controlled_by = owner
			}
			factor = 0.1
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			PAP = {
				clr_country_flag = church_council_topics_chosen
				clr_country_flag = council_site_chosen
				clr_country_flag = church_council
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.059.a
		remove_province_modifier = church_council
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_province_flag = church_council
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_prestige = -3
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_prestige = -2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_prestige = -1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = attend_council
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.60
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = council_failed_fanatical
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.20
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = council_failed_pious
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.20
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = council_failed_observant
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = attend_council
			}
			PAP = {
				clr_country_flag = council_accomplishments
				clr_country_flag = church_council
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
					OR = {
						is_papal_controller = yes
						tag = PAP
						AND = {
							religion = catholic
							has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = dg_catholic.113
					days = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = dg_catholic.061
	title = dg_catholic.061.t
	desc = dg_catholic.061.d
	picture = catholic_trial
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = renaissance
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = catholic_corruption
					value = 4
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = great_matter
			set_country_flag = royal_scandal
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_religion_enabled = protestant
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = protestant_reaction
					}
					has_country_flag = renaissance
				}
				clr_country_flag = renaissance
				capital_scope = {
					clr_country_flag = renaissance_ideas
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.061.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = religious_scandal_country
				duration = 800
			}
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_scandal_province
					duration = 1600
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = religious_scandal_country
				duration = 400
			}
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_scandal_province
					duration = 800
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = religious_scandal_country
				duration = 200
			}
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_scandal_province
					duration = 400
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = religious_scandal_country
				duration = 100
			}
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_scandal_province
					duration = 200
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_legitimacy = -10
			add_devotion = -20
			add_republican_tradition = -5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_legitimacy = -8
			add_devotion = -16
			add_republican_tradition = -4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_legitimacy = -6
			add_devotion = -12
			add_republican_tradition = -3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_legitimacy = -4
			add_devotion = -8
			add_republican_tradition = -2
		}
		else = {
			add_legitimacy = -2
			add_devotion = -4
			add_republican_tradition = -1
		}
	}
}

					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = denied_heretic_alliance

				}

			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = excommunication_blasphemy
			}
			set_country_flag = catholic_blasphemy
		}
		set_country_flag = excommunicated
		clr_country_flag = repress_protestants_abroad
		clr_country_flag = counter_reformation
		clr_country_flag = catholic_reformation
		clr_country_flag = reaction_to_reformation
		clr_country_flag = reformation_maybe
		clr_country_flag = introduce_reformation
		clr_country_flag = spread_reformation
		clr_country_flag = refused_reformation
		clr_country_flag = renaissance
		set_country_flag = former_excommunication_target
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = christian
				NOT = {
					tag = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					war_with = ROOT
					alliance_with = ROOT
					junior_union_with = ROOT
					senior_union_with = ROOT
					vassal_of = ROOT
					overlord_of = ROOT
					has_country_flag = religious_news_all
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
						OR = {
							is_neighbor_of = ROOT
							marriage_with = ROOT
							truce_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					AND = {
						religion = catholic
						OR = {
							ai = yes
							has_country_flag = religious_news_major
						}
						OR = {
							is_defender_of_faith = yes
							is_neighbor_of = ROOT
							has_country_flag = religious_news_trivial
							AND = {
								OR = {
									has_reform = papacy_reform
									has_reform = papal_government
								}
							}
							is_papal_controller = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = dg_catholic.080
				days = 30
			}
		}
		add_papal_influence = -10
		if = {
			limit = {
				advisor = theologian
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				remove_advisor = theologian
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				advisor = inquisitor
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				remove_advisor = inquisitor
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						religion = protestant
						religion = reformed
					}
					PAP = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = first_reformation
						}
					}
				}
				PAP = {
					set_country_flag = first_reformation
				}
				AVI = {
					set_country_flag = first_reformation
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					PAP = {
						check_variable = {
							which = papal_authority
							value = 500
						}
					}
				}
				add_stability = -2
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						id = POP_Stability.003
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_emperor_of_china = yes
					}
					add_mandate = -10
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					PAP = {
						check_variable = {
							which = papal_authority
							value = 400
						}
					}
				}
				add_stability = -1
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						id = POP_Stability.003
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_emperor_of_china = yes
					}
					add_mandate = -5
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					PAP = {
						check_variable = {
							which = papal_authority
							value = 300
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = stability_points_lost_50
				hidden_effect = {
					subtract_variable = {
						which = stability_points
						value = 50
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								check_variable = {
									which = stability_points
									value = 0
								}
							}
						}
						add_stability = -1
						country_event = {
							id = POP_Stability.003
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_emperor_of_china = yes
							}
							add_mandate = -5
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = religious_scandal_country
					duration = 4000
				}
				add_prestige = -8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = religious_scandal_country
					duration = 2000
				}
				add_prestige = -6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = religious_scandal_country
					duration = 1000
				}
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = religious_scandal_country
					duration = 500
				}
				add_prestige = -2
			}
			else = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = religious_scandal_country
					duration = 250
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_prestige = -8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_prestige = -6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_prestige = -2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = excommunication_charges
				value = 0
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_papal_controller = yes
				}
				set_country_flag = excommunication_excommunicated
				country_event = {
					id = dg_pope.028
					days = 30
				}
			}
		}
	}

						num_of_cities = ROOT
					}
				}
				add_legitimacy = -0.5
				add_prestige = -4
			}
			else = {
				add_prestige = -2
			}
		}
		add_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = marriage_broken
		}
		FROM = {
			break_marriage = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_idea_group = diplomatic_ideas
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						custom_tooltip = stability_points_gained_50
						hidden_effect = {
							change_variable = {
								which = stability_points
								value = 50
							}
							country_event = {
								id = POP_Stability.002
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = ROOT
				}
				PREV = {
					add_casus_belli = {
						target = FROM
						months = 240
						type = cb_restore_personal_union
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				PREV = {
					add_casus_belli = {
						target = FROM
						months = 240
						type = cb_annulment
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

							who = ROOT
							modifier = rival_popes_fanatical
						}

							who = ROOT
							modifier = rival_popes_pious
						}

							who = ROOT
							modifier = rival_popes_observant
						}
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = rival_popes_decadent
						}
					}
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = rival_popes_fanatical
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = rival_popes_pious
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = rival_popes_observant
				}

					who = ROOT
					modifier = rival_popes_decadent
				}

					who = ROOT
					modifier = rival_popes_fanatical
				}

					who = ROOT
					modifier = rival_popes_pious
				}

		}

				}

		}

				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_prestige = 4
		}
		else_if = {

			add_prestige = 3
		}
		else_if = {

			add_prestige = 2

		else_if = {

			add_prestige = 1

country_event = {
	id = dg_catholic.141
	title = dg_catholic.141.t
	desc = dg_catholic.141.d
	picture = catholic_jesuit_mission
	trigger = {
		religion = catholic
		check_variable = {
			which = jesuit_support
			value = 1
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_proposed
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = jesuits_suppressed
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = jesuits_expelled
		}
		any_known_country = {
			NOT = {
				religion_group = christian
			}
			NOT = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
			NOT = {
				religion_group = jewish_group
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = theology
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 41
		modifier = {
			PAP = {
				has_country_flag = jesuits_limited
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.60
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			piety = 0.20
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			patriarch_authority = 0.75
			factor = 0.7
		}
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.25
			}
			factor = 1.4
		}
		modifier = {
			num_of_colonies = 1
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			colony = 1
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			any_neighbor_country = {
				NOT = {
					religion_group = christian
				}

		name = dg_catholic.141.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}

		set_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
		if = {
			limit = {

		}
		else_if = {

				monthly_income = 4
			}

		}

				duration = 2000
			}
		}

			limit = {

			}
			add_country_modifier = {

				duration = 1000
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				patriarch_authority = 0.25
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = theology
				duration = 500
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = theology
				duration = 250
			}
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {

				}
				NOT = {
					base_tax = 6
				}

					owner = {
						NOT = {
							religion_group = christian
						}
						NOT = {
							religion_group = muslim
						}
						NOT = {
							religion_group = jewish_group
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_province_flag = university_present
					}
				}
				num_free_building_slots = 1
			}
			add_building = small_university
		}

					check_variable = {
						which = catholic
						value = 6
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_riots
					duration = 300
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = catholic
						value = 4
					}
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_riots
					duration = 200
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = religious_riots
					duration = 100
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.145.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = minority_usefulness
				value = 60
			}
			set_country_flag = useful_catholic
		}
		set_country_flag = jesuit_missions_allowed
		add_stability = -1
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = POP_Stability.003
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_emperor_of_china = yes
			}
			add_mandate = -5
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_owner_religion = yes
				check_variable = {
					which = catholic
					value = 2
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = religious_riots
				duration = 500
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = catholic
					value = 2
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = catholic_10
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = {
					which = catholic
					value = 2
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = province_religion
					value = -2
				}
			}
			random_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = catholic
							value = 2
						}
					}
					owned_by = ROOT
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					change_variable = {
						which = catholic
						value = 2
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = province_religion
						value = -2
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = missionary_sponsor_strong
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				random_active_trade_node = {
					limit = {
						strongest_trade_power = {
							tag = ROOT
						}
					}
					add_trade_modifier = {
						who = PREV
						duration = 4000
						power = 10
						key = minority_contacts
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = aided_coreligionists_fanatical
			}
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = catholic
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_supported
				}
				has_country_flag = jesuit_missions_encouraged
			}
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = missionary_sponsor_weak
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				random_active_trade_node = {
					limit = {
						strongest_trade_power = {
							tag = ROOT
						}
					}
					add_trade_modifier = {
						who = PREV
						duration = 4000
						power = 5
						key = minority_contacts
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = aided_coreligionists_pious
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = dg_catholic.146
	title = dg_catholic.146.t
	desc = dg_catholic.146.d
	picture = catholic_jesuits_asia
	trigger = {
		religion = catholic
		has_country_flag = black_robes_arrived
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = true_catholic
		}
		NOT = {
			capital_scope = {
				continent = europe
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			is_colonial_nation = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			is_former_colonial_nation = yes
		}
		is_force_converted = no
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 8
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.146.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		set_country_flag = true_catholic
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.146.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_stability = -1
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = POP_Stability.003
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_emperor_of_china = yes
			}
			add_mandate = -5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							continent = southeast_asia
							continent = indian_continent
							continent = east_asia
							continent = central_asia
							continent = north_asia
						}
					}
				}
			}
			change_religion = chaldean
			force_converted = yes
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = catholic
						value = 2
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = chaldean
					which = catholic
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = catholic
					value = 0
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							superregion = east_africa_superregion
							superregion = west_africa_superregion
							superregion = north_africa_superregion
							region = egypt_region
						}
					}
				}
			}
			change_religion = coptic
			force_converted = yes
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = catholic
						value = 2
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = coptic
					which = catholic
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = catholic
					value = 0
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			change_religion = gnostic
			force_converted = yes
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = catholic
						value = 2
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = gnostic
					which = catholic
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = catholic
					value = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
province_event = {
	id = dg_catholic.161
	title = dg_catholic.161.t
	desc = dg_catholic.161.d
	picture = catholic_bishop
	trigger = {
		has_province_modifier = catholic_patriarchate
		NOT = {
			has_province_flag = orthodox_pentarchy
		}
		owner = {
			religion = catholic
			num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
				has_province_modifier = catholic_patriarchate
				NOT = {
					has_province_flag = orthodox_pentarchy
				}
				culture_group = ROOT
				value = 2
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 25
		modifier = {
			is_capital = yes
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			factor = 0.5
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		set_province_flag = rival_latin_patriarch
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.161.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		owner = {
			add_papal_influence = 100
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_prestige = 10
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_prestige = 8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_prestige = 6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_prestige = 4
			}
			else = {
				add_prestige = 2
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = catholic_patriarchate
					NOT = {
						has_province_flag = orthodox_pentarchy
					}
					culture_group = ROOT
				}
				clr_province_flag = catholic_patriarchate
				set_province_flag = catholic_archbishopric
				remove_province_modifier = catholic_patriarchate
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = catholic_archbishopric
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_catholic.161.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				is_capital = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_owner_culture = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_papal_influence = 100
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_prestige = 10
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_prestige = 8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_prestige = 6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_prestige = 4
			}
			else = {
				add_prestige = 2
			}
		}
		clr_province_flag = catholic_patriarchate
		set_province_flag = catholic_archbishopric
		remove_province_modifier = catholic_patriarchate
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = catholic_archbishopric
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}
